## Q3
mit kene csinalni  hogy a futhark gpu raf is 100% ban a sajat root archetikurat kovesse mint a Zog?
### Answer
The user is asking what needs to be done so that the Futhark GPU path also follows 100% the same root architecture as the Zig side. I already identified the inconsistency in the previous conversation - the `main.fut` uses relu and layer_norm while the Zig `rsf.zig` uses pure affine coupling.

Let me look at the specific files involved to give a precise answer about what needs to change:
1. `main.fut` - the GPU entry points that need to be rewritten
2. `futhark_kernels.fut` - which already has the correct `rsf_forward_layer` (scatter + flow)
3. `accel_interface.zig` - the Zig bindings that call the Futhark entries

Let me read these files in full to understand exactly what needs to change.



Now I have a complete picture. Let me also check the futhark_bindings.zig to see the exact entry point signatures for the main.fut rsf_forward, and also check if there are any other callers of these functions.

The key issue is clear:

1. **`main.fut`** has its own `rsf_forward` entry that uses `relu` and `layer_norm` - this is the f16 2D GPU path
2. **`futhark_kernels.fut`** has its own `rsf_forward` entry (line 385) that uses `rsf_forward_layer` (scatter + flow) - this is the f32 1D path

Wait, there's a naming conflict! Both files have an `entry rsf_forward`. Let me check the bindings to see which one is actually used.

Looking at `futhark_bindings.zig` line references from earlier context, it has:
- `futhark_entry_rsf_forward` - but which file does this come from?

The `main.fut` rsf_forward takes `[n][d]f16` (2D f16 arrays) and returns `[n][d]f16`
The `futhark_kernels.fut` rsf_forward takes `[n]f32` (1D f32 arrays) and returns `[n]f32`

These are different entry points with different signatures. The `RSFAccelerator.forward()` calls `futhark_entry_rsf_forward` with f16_2d arrays, so it's calling the `main.fut` version.

Let me check the futhark_bindings.zig to confirm.



Now I have the complete picture. Let me analyze what needs to change.

The key finding is:

1. **`futhark_bindings.zig` line 73** declares `futhark_entry_rsf_forward` with `f16_2d` signature — this maps to `main.fut`'s `rsf_forward` (which uses relu + layer_norm)
2. **`futhark_kernels.fut` line 385** also has an `entry rsf_forward` but with `f32_1d` signature (scatter + flow) — this is a different entry point
3. The `RSFAccelerator.forward()` calls the f16_2d version (main.fut), which is the relu + layer_norm path

So the `main.fut` file is the problematic one. It needs to be rewritten to use the same affine coupling logic as the Zig `rsf.zig`.

Let me also check if `compute_rsf_context` is called from Zig anywhere, since it uses softmax internally.

Looking at the grep results, `compute_rsf_context` only appears in `futhark_kernels.fut` and the generated C files (`futhark_kernels.c`, `futhark_kernels.h`). It's not referenced from any Zig file, so it's an exposed entry point but not currently called from the Zig side.

Now let me formulate the complete answer about what needs to change to make the Futhark GPU path 100% consistent with the Zig RSF architecture.

The changes needed:

### 1. `main.fut` — Complete rewrite of `rsf_forward`

Current (broken):
```futhark
entry rsf_forward [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_s: [d][d]f16) (weights_t: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  let after_spectral = rsf_spectral_transform input weights_s
  let after_relu1 = relu after_spectral
  let after_temporal = rsf_temporal_transform after_relu1 weights_t
  let after_relu2 = relu after_temporal
  in layer_norm after_relu2
```

This needs to be rewritten to implement the same affine coupling as `rsf.zig`:
1. Split each row into x1 (first half) and x2 (second half)
2. Compute scale: s = exp(clip(W_s · x2 + b_s))
3. y1 = x1 * s
4. Compute translation: t = W_t · y1 + b_t
5. y2 = x2 + t
6. Concatenate y1, y2

But wait — the `main.fut` signature is different from the Zig path. The `main.fut` takes `weights_s: [d][d]f16` and `weights_t: [d][d]f16` as 2D matrices, while the `futhark_kernels.fut` `rsf_forward_layer` takes 1D arrays for weights plus permutation indices.

The changes needed are:

### A. Rewrite `main.fut`

The `rsf_forward` entry needs to implement the affine coupling logic:
- Split input rows into halves
- Apply exp(clip(W_s · x2 + b_s)) for scale
- Multiply x1 by scale
- Apply W_t · y1 + b_t for translation
- Add translation to x2

Also need to add:
- `clip_min` and `clip_max` parameters (or hardcode defaults like -5.0, 5.0)
- `s_bias` and `t_bias` parameters
- `perm_indices` for the scatter operation

### B. Update `futhark_bindings.zig`

The `futhark_entry_rsf_forward` signature needs to change to accept the new parameters (biases, clip values, permutation indices).

### C. Update `RSFAccelerator` in `accel_interface.zig`

The `RSFAccelerator` struct needs to store the additional parameters (biases, clip values, permutation indices) and pass them to the updated Futhark entry.

### D. The gradient functions also need updating

`rsf_grad_spectral` and `rsf_grad_temporal` in `main.fut` compute simple matrix gradients — they need to be replaced with the affine coupling backward pass (similar to `rsf_backward_layer` in `futhark_kernels.fut`).

### E. `rsf_relational_context` in `futhark_kernels.fut`

This uses inline softmax and layer_norm. If the goal is 100% purity, this needs to be rewritten too. But it's not currently called from Zig, so it's lower priority.

### F. The `relu` and `layer_norm` entries in `main.fut` can be removed

They're only used by `rsf_forward` in `main.fut`. The standalone `apply_relu`, `apply_layer_norm` etc. in `futhark_kernels.fut` are separate entry points used by `GPUOps`.

### G. The `GPUOps` utility functions

`GPUOps.softmax()`, `GPUOps.layerNorm()`, `GPUOps.relu()`, `GPUOps.gelu()` — these are standalone utility functions. They could be kept as general-purpose GPU utilities even if the RSF core doesn't use them. But if the goal is absolute purity, they could be removed too.

Let me now write a clear, structured answer in Hungarian.


A `main.fut` GPU útvonal és a Zig-oldali `rsf.zig` között **két teljesen különböző architektúra** fut. Íme pontosan mi kell ahhoz, hogy a GPU útvonal is 100%-ban a saját RSF architektúrát kövesse:

---

## A probléma gyökere

A `futhark_bindings.zig` 73. sorában deklarált `futhark_entry_rsf_forward` az **f16 2D** szignátúrával a `main.fut` fájlra mutat: kissofdeath:73-74 

Ez a `main.fut`-beli `rsf_forward`-ot hívja, ami `spectral_transform → relu → temporal_transform → relu → layer_norm`: kissofdeath:29-34 

Közben a `futhark_kernels.fut`-ban **már létezik** a helyes, tiszta RSF implementáció (`rsf_forward_layer` = scatter + flow), de az f32 1D szignátúrával: kissofdeath:385-386 

---

## Konkrétan mit kell csinálni

### 1. `main.fut` — Az `rsf_forward` átírása

A jelenlegi pipeline:
```futhark
-- JELENLEGI (hibás — relu + layer_norm):
entry rsf_forward [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_s: [d][d]f16) (weights_t: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  let after_spectral = rsf_spectral_transform input weights_s
  let after_relu1 = relu after_spectral
  let after_temporal = rsf_temporal_transform after_relu1 weights_t
  let after_relu2 = relu after_temporal
  in layer_norm after_relu2
``` kissofdeath:29-34 

Ezt le kell cserélni a Zig `rsf.zig` `forwardInPlace` logikájára, ami:
1. Minden sort kettéoszt: `x1 = row[0..half]`, `x2 = row[half..d]`
2. Scale: `s = exp(clip(W_s · x2 + b_s, clip_min, clip_max))`
3. `y1 = x1 * s` (elemenként)
4. Translation: `t = W_t · y1 + b_t`
5. `y2 = x2 + t` (elemenként)
6. Összefűzés: `row = y1 ++ y2` kissofdeath:371-398 

Az új szignátúrának tartalmaznia kell a **bias vektorokat** és a **clip paramétereket** is:

```futhark
-- ÚJ (helyes — tiszta affin coupling):
entry rsf_forward [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) 
  (weights_s: [d/2][d/2]f16) (weights_t: [d/2][d/2]f16)
  (s_bias: [d/2]f16) (t_bias: [d/2]f16)
  (clip_min: f16) (clip_max: f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  map (\row ->
    let half = d / 2
    let x1 = row[0:half]
    let x2 = row[half:d]
    -- Scale
    let scale = map2 (\j bias ->
      let sum = bias + f16.sum (map2 (*) weights_s[j] x2)
      let clipped = f16.max clip_min (f16.min clip_max sum)
      in f16.exp clipped
    ) (iota half) s_bias
    -- y1 = x1 * scale
    let y1 = map2 (*) x1 scale
    -- Translation
    let trans = map2 (\j bias ->
      bias + f16.sum (map2 (*) weights_t[j] y1)
    ) (iota half) t_bias
    -- y2 = x2 + trans
    let y2 = map2 (+) x2 trans
    in y1 ++ y2
  ) input
```

### 2. `main.fut` — A gradient függvények átírása

Az `rsf_grad_spectral` és `rsf_grad_temporal` jelenleg egyszerű mátrix-gradienseket számolnak: kissofdeath:36-53 

Ezeket le kell cserélni az affin coupling backward logikájára, ami a `rsf.zig` `backwardFromOutputs`-nak felel meg — a kimenetből rekonstruálja a bemenetet (y2 - t → x2, y1 / s → x1), majd kiszámolja a gradienseket: kissofdeath:490-549 

A `futhark_kernels.fut`-ban az `rsf_backward_layer` már tartalmazza a helyes backward logikát — ezt lehet mintaként használni: kissofdeath:201-207 

### 3. `main.fut` — A `relu` és `layer_norm` entry-k törlése

Ezek a `main.fut`-ban kizárólag az `rsf_forward`-hoz kellettek. Az átírás után törölhetők: kissofdeath:17-27 

Az `rsf_spectral_transform` és `rsf_temporal_transform` is törölhetők, mert azok egyszerű mátrixszorzások voltak, amiket az affin coupling logika vált ki: kissofdeath:3-15 

### 4. `main.fut` — A `training_step` és `batch_forward` automatikusan javul

Mivel a `batch_forward` a `rsf_forward`-ot hívja, és a `training_step` a `batch_forward`-ot, ezek automatikusan a helyes logikát fogják használni az átírás után: kissofdeath:68-69 kissofdeath:97-114 

### 5. `futhark_bindings.zig` — Szignátúra frissítés

A `futhark_entry_rsf_forward` extern deklarációt frissíteni kell az új paraméterekkel (bias-ok, clip értékek): kissofdeath:73-74 

```zig
// ÚJ szignátúra:

    ctx: ?*struct_futhark_context, 
    out: ?*?*struct_futhark_f16_2d,

    t_bias: ?*struct_futhark_f16_1d,
    clip_min: f16,
    clip_max: f16,
) c_int;
```

Ugyanígy a `futhark_entry_training_step` szignátúrája is frissítendő: kissofdeath:76-91 

### 6. `accel_interface.zig` — `RSFAccelerator` bővítése

Az `RSFAccelerator` struct-nak tárolnia kell a bias-okat és clip értékeket: kissofdeath:344-382

### 7. (Opcionális) `futhark_kernels.fut` — `rsf_relational_context` tisztítása

Az `rsf_relational_context` belül inline softmax-ot és normalizációt használ. Jelenleg **nincs Zig-oldali hívója** (csak a `futhark_kernels.c/h`-ban van exportálva), de ha 100%-os tisztaságot akarsz, ezt is át kellene írni: kissofdeath:287-330 

### 8. (Opcionális) `GPUOps` utility-k megtartása

A `GPUOps.softmax()`, `.layerNorm()`, `.relu()`, `.gelu()` standalone GPU utility-k. Ezek **nem az RSF pipeline részei**, hanem általános célú GPU műveletek. Megtarthatók mint utility-k, vagy törölhetők ha a teljes Futhark kódbázist tisztítani akarod: kissofdeath:624-686

entry rsf_spectral_transform [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_s: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  map (\row ->
    map (\j ->
      f16.sum (map2 (\x w -> x f16.* w) row weights_s[j])
    ) (iota d)
  ) input

entry rsf_temporal_transform [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_t: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  map (\row ->
    map (\j ->
      f16.sum (map2 (\x w -> x f16.* w) row weights_t[j])
    ) (iota d)
  ) input

**File:** src/hw/accel/main.fut (L17-27)
```text
entry relu [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  map (map (\x -> f16.max x (f16.i32 0))) input

entry layer_norm [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  let epsilon = f16.f32 1e-5
  in map (\row ->
    let mean = (f16.sum row) f16./ (f16.i64 d)
    let variance = (f16.sum (map (\x -> (x f16.- mean) f16.* (x f16.- mean)) row)) f16./ (f16.i64 d)
    let std_dev = f16.sqrt (variance f16.+ epsilon)
    in map (\x -> (x f16.- mean) f16./ std_dev) row
  ) input
```
**File:** src/hw/accel/main.fut (L29-34)

entry rsf_forward [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_s: [d][d]f16) (weights_t: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  let after_spectral = rsf_spectral_transform input weights_s
  let after_relu1 = relu after_spectral
  let after_temporal = rsf_temporal_transform after_relu1 weights_t
  let after_relu2 = relu after_temporal
  in layer_norm after_relu2
```

```text
entry rsf_grad_spectral [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (grad_output: [n][d]f16) : *[d][d]f16 =
  let grad_weights = replicate d (replicate d (f16.i32 0))
  in loop grad_weights for i < n do
       loop grad_weights for j < d do
         loop grad_weights for k < d do
           let update = input[i,k] f16.* grad_output[i,j]
           let grad_weights[j,k] = grad_weights[j,k] f16.+ update
           in grad_weights

entry rsf_grad_temporal [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (grad_output: [n][d]f16) : *[d][d]f16 =
  let grad_weights = replicate d (replicate d (f16.i32 0))
  in loop grad_weights for i < n do
       loop grad_weights for j < d do
         loop grad_weights for k < d do
           let update = input[i,k] f16.* grad_output[i,j]
           let grad_weights[j,k] = grad_weights[j,k] f16.+ update
           in grad_weights

```

```text
entry training_step [batch_size][seq_len][d] 
  (inputs: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16)
  (targets: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16)
  (weights_s: *[d][d]f16)
  (weights_t: *[d][d]f16)
  (velocity_s: *[d][d]f16)
  (velocity_t: *[d][d]f16)
  (learning_rate: f16)
  (momentum: f16) : (*[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16, f16) =

  let outputs = batch_forward inputs weights_s weights_t
  let loss = batch_compute_loss outputs targets
  let grad_outputs = map2 (map2 (map2 (\o t -> (f16.f32 2.0) f16.* (o f16.- t)))) outputs targets
  let (grad_s, grad_t) = batch_gradients inputs grad_outputs
  let (new_weights_s, new_velocity_s) = sfd_update weights_s grad_s learning_rate momentum velocity_s
  let (new_weights_t, new_velocity_t) = sfd_update weights_t grad_t learning_rate momentum velocity_t

  in (new_weights_s, new_weights_t, new_velocity_s, new_velocity_t, loss)
```

```text
let rsf_backward_layer [n] (grad_out: [n]f32) (x: [n]f32) (s_weight: [n]f32) (t_weight: [n]f32) (perm_indices: [n]i64): ([n]f32, [n]f32, [n]f32, [n]f32, [n]f32) =
  if n < 2 then (copy grad_out, replicate n 0f32, replicate n 0f32, replicate n 0f32, replicate n 0f32)
  else
    let scattered_x = rsf_scatter x perm_indices
    let (grad_flow, grad_s_w, grad_t_w, grad_s_b, grad_t_b) = rsf_backward_flow grad_out scattered_x s_weight t_weight
    let grad_x = rsf_backward_scatter grad_flow perm_indices
    in (grad_x, grad_s_w, grad_t_w, grad_s_b, grad_t_b)

**File:** src/hw/accel/futhark_kernels.fut (L287-330)
```text
let rsf_relational_context [seq_len][d_model] (spectral_input: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (temporal_input: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (value: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (s_weight: [d_model]f32) (t_weight: [d_model]f32) (eps: f32): [seq_len][d_model]f32 =
  if seq_len == 0 || d_model == 0 then copy value
  else
    let safe_eps = f32.max eps 1e-12f32
    let inv_sqrt_d = 1f32 / f32.sqrt (f32.max 1f32 (f32.i64 d_model))
    let s_sum = reduce (+) 0f32 s_weight
    let t_sum = reduce (+) 0f32 t_weight
    let residual_scale = (s_sum + t_sum) * inv_sqrt_d * inv_sqrt_d
    let spectral_scores = map (\row ->
      let weighted = map2 (*) row s_weight
      in tabulate seq_len (\j ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (*) weighted value[j]) * inv_sqrt_d
      )
    ) spectral_input
    let temporal_scores = map (\row ->
      let weighted = map2 (*) row t_weight
      in tabulate seq_len (\j ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (*) weighted value[j]) * inv_sqrt_d
      )
    ) temporal_input
    let relational_weights = map2 (\s_row t_row ->
      let combined = map2 (+) s_row t_row
      let max_v = reduce f32.max (-f32.inf) combined
      let exp_vals = map (\xi -> f32.exp (xi - max_v)) combined
      let total = reduce (+) 0f32 exp_vals
      in (if total <= 0f32 || f32.isnan total
         then replicate seq_len (1f32 / f32.i64 seq_len)
         else map (\e -> e / total) exp_vals) :> [seq_len]f32
    ) spectral_scores temporal_scores
    let output = map (\weights ->
      tabulate d_model (\d ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (\w j -> w * value[j, d]) weights (iota seq_len))
      )
    ) relational_weights
    let with_residual = map2 (\out_row inp_row ->
      map2 (\o xi -> o + xi * residual_scale) out_row inp_row
    ) output spectral_input
    in map (\row ->
      let row_mean = (reduce (+) 0f32 row) / f32.i64 d_model
      let centered = map (\xi -> xi - row_mean) row
      let variance = (reduce (+) 0f32 (map (\c -> c * c) centered)) / f32.i64 d_model
      let row_std = f32.sqrt (f32.max variance 0f32 + safe_eps)
      in map (\c -> c / row_std) centered
    ) with_residual
```

**File:** src/processor/rsf.zig (L371-398)
```text
    fn forwardInPlace(self: *const LayerCore, x1: *Tensor, x2: *Tensor) !void {
        if (tensorsOverlap(x1, x2)) return error.AliasedBuffers;
        const batch_size = try self.validatePair(x1, x2);
        var stack_fallback = std.heap.stackFallback(4096, scratchAllocator());
        const allocator = stack_fallback.get();

        const scale = try allocator.alloc(f32, self.dim);
        defer allocator.free(scale);

        const trans = try allocator.alloc(f32, self.dim);
        defer allocator.free(trans);

        var b: usize = 0;
        while (b < batch_size) : (b += 1) {
            const x1_row = x1.data[b * self.dim .. b * self.dim + self.dim];
            const x2_row = x2.data[b * self.dim .. b * self.dim + self.dim];

            self.computeScaleRow(x2_row, scale);

            var i: usize = 0;
            while (i < self.dim) : (i += 1) x1_row[i] *= scale[i];

            self.computeTranslationRow(x1_row, trans);

            i = 0;
            while (i < self.dim) : (i += 1) x2_row[i] += trans[i];
        }
    }

        b = 0;
        while (b < batch_size) : (b += 1) {
            const y1_row = y1.data[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            const y2_row = y2.data[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            const x2_row = x2_out.data[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            const x1_row = x1_out.data[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            const dx1_row = dx1_out.data[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            const ds_row = ds[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            const dy1_total_row = dy1_total[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];

            var d: usize = 0;
            while (d < dim) : (d += 1) {
                var trans_sum: f32 = self.t_bias.data[d];
                const t_row = self.t_weight.data[d * dim .. d * dim + dim];
                var j: usize = 0;
                while (j < dim) : (j += 1) trans_sum += t_row[j] * y1_row[j];
                x2_row[d] = y2_row[d] - trans_sum;
            }

            var d2: usize = 0;
            while (d2 < dim) : (d2 += 1) {
                var pre_sum: f32 = self.s_bias.data[d2];
                const s_row = self.s_weight.data[d2 * dim .. d2 * dim + dim];
                var j2: usize = 0;
                while (j2 < dim) : (j2 += 1) pre_sum += s_row[j2] * x2_row[j2];

                const clipped = if (pre_sum < self.clip_min) self.clip_min else if (pre_sum > self.clip_max) self.clip_max else pre_sum;
                const scale = @exp(clipped);

                x1_row[d2] = y1_row[d2] / scale;
                dx1_row[d2] = dy1_total_row[d2] * scale;
                ds_row[d2] = if (pre_sum < self.clip_min or pre_sum > self.clip_max) 0.0 else dy1_total_row[d2] * y1_row[d2];
            }

            if (self.s_weight_grad) |*swg| {
                var d3: usize = 0;
                while (d3 < dim) : (d3 += 1) {
                    const dsv = ds_row[d3] * grad_scale;
                    var j3: usize = 0;
                    while (j3 < dim) : (j3 += 1) swg.data[d3 * dim + j3] += dsv * x2_row[j3];
                }
            }

            if (self.s_bias_grad) |*sbg| {
                var d4: usize = 0;
                while (d4 < dim) : (d4 += 1) sbg.data[d4] += ds_row[d4] * grad_scale;
            }

            const dx2_row = dx2_out.data[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            const dy2_row = dy2_in.data[b * dim .. b * dim + dim];
            @memcpy(dx2_row, dy2_row);
            var d5: usize = 0;
            while (d5 < dim) : (d5 += 1) {
                const ds_val = ds_row[d5];
                const s_row = self.s_weight.data[d5 * dim .. d5 * dim + dim];
                var j4: usize = 0;
                while (j4 < dim) : (j4 += 1) dx2_row[j4] += s_row[j4] * ds_val;
            }
        }
    }

```text
pub const RSFAccelerator = struct {
    ctx: FutharkContext,
    weights_s: FutharkArray2DF16,
    weights_t: FutharkArray2DF16,
    velocity_s: FutharkArray2DF16,
    velocity_t: FutharkArray2DF16,
    model_dim: usize,
    initialized: bool,

    const Self = @This();

    pub fn init(model_dim: usize) AccelError!Self {
        if (model_dim == 0) return AccelError.InvalidDimensions;

        var ctx = try FutharkContext.init();
        errdefer ctx.deinit();

        var weights_s = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer weights_s.free(&ctx);

        var weights_t = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer weights_t.free(&ctx);

        var velocity_s = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer velocity_s.free(&ctx);

        var velocity_t = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer velocity_t.free(&ctx);

        return Self{
            .ctx = ctx,
            .weights_s = weights_s,
            .weights_t = weights_t,
            .velocity_s = velocity_s,
            .velocity_t = velocity_t,
            .model_dim = model_dim,
            .initialized = true,
        };
    }

**File:** src/hw/accel/accel_interface.zig (L395-424)
```text
    pub fn forward(self: *Self, input: *FutharkArray2DF16) AccelError!FutharkArray2DF16 {
        if (!self.initialized) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (self.ctx.ctx == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (input.arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (self.weights_s.arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (self.weights_t.arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var output: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f16_2d = null;
        const result = futhark.futhark_entry_rsf_forward(
            self.ctx.ctx,
            &output,
            input.arr,
            self.weights_s.arr,
            self.weights_t.arr,
        );

        if (result != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkForwardFailed;
        }

        if (output == null) {
            return AccelError.NullPointer;
        }

        return FutharkArray2DF16{
            .arr = output,
            .rows = input.rows,
            .cols = input.cols,
        };
    }

**File:** src/hw/accel/accel_interface.zig (L426-490)
```text
    pub fn trainingStep(
        self: *Self,
        inputs: *FutharkArray2DF16,
        targets: *FutharkArray2DF16,
        learning_rate: f16,
        momentum: f16,
    ) AccelError!f16 {
        if (!self.initialized) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (self.ctx.ctx == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (inputs.arr == null or targets.arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (self.weights_s.arr == null or self.weights_t.arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;
        if (self.velocity_s.arr == null or self.velocity_t.arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var new_ws: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f16_2d = null;
        var new_wt: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f16_2d = null;
        var new_vs: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f16_2d = null;
        var new_vt: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f16_2d = null;
        var loss: u16 = 0;

        const lr_bits: u16 = @bitCast(learning_rate);
        const momentum_bits: u16 = @bitCast(momentum);

        const result = futhark.futhark_entry_training_step(
            self.ctx.ctx,
            &new_ws,
            &new_wt,
            &new_vs,
            &new_vt,
            &loss,
            inputs.arr,
            targets.arr,
            self.weights_s.arr,
            self.weights_t.arr,
            self.velocity_s.arr,
            self.velocity_t.arr,
            lr_bits,
            momentum_bits,
        );

        if (result != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkTrainingStepFailed;
        }

        if (new_ws == null or new_wt == null or new_vs == null or new_vt == null) {
            return AccelError.NullPointer;
        }

        const old_ws = self.weights_s.arr;
        const old_wt = self.weights_t.arr;
        const old_vs = self.velocity_s.arr;
        const old_vt = self.velocity_t.arr;

        self.weights_s.arr = new_ws;
        self.weights_t.arr = new_wt;
        self.velocity_s.arr = new_vs;
        self.velocity_t.arr = new_vt;

        _ = futhark.futhark_free_f16_2d(self.ctx.ctx, old_ws);
        _ = futhark.futhark_free_f16_2d(self.ctx.ctx, old_wt);
        _ = futhark.futhark_free_f16_2d(self.ctx.ctx, old_vs);
        _ = futhark.futhark_free_f16_2d(self.ctx.ctx, old_vt);

        const loss_f16: f16 = @bitCast(loss);
        return loss_f16;
    }
```

```text
    pub fn softmax(self: *Self, input: *const core_tensor.Tensor, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) AccelError!core_tensor.Tensor {
        var fi = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, input);
        defer fi.free(&self.ctx);

        var out_arr: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f32_1d = null;
        if (futhark.futhark_entry_apply_softmax(self.ctx.ctx, &out_arr, fi.arr) != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkForwardFailed;
        }
        if (out_arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var result = FutharkArray1DF32{ .arr = out_arr, .len = input.shape.dims[0] };
        defer result.free(&self.ctx);
        return result.toTensor(&self.ctx, allocator);
    }

    pub fn layerNorm(self: *Self, input: *const core_tensor.Tensor, gamma: *const core_tensor.Tensor, beta: *const core_tensor.Tensor, eps: f32, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) AccelError!core_tensor.Tensor {
        var fi = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, input);
        defer fi.free(&self.ctx);
        var fg = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, gamma);
        defer fg.free(&self.ctx);
        var fb = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, beta);
        defer fb.free(&self.ctx);

        var out_arr: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f32_1d = null;
        if (futhark.futhark_entry_apply_layer_norm(self.ctx.ctx, &out_arr, fi.arr, fg.arr, fb.arr, eps) != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkForwardFailed;
        }
        if (out_arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var result = FutharkArray1DF32{ .arr = out_arr, .len = input.shape.dims[0] };
        defer result.free(&self.ctx);
        return result.toTensor(&self.ctx, allocator);
    }

    pub fn relu(self: *Self, input: *const core_tensor.Tensor, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) AccelError!core_tensor.Tensor {

        defer result.free(&self.ctx);
        return result.toTensor(&self.ctx, allocator);
    }

Now let me categorize these findings:

### Critical (part of actual inference/training pipeline):

1. **`main.fut` `rsf_forward`** — Uses `relu` + `layer_norm` in the GPU forward pass. **CRITICAL** — already discussed.

2. **`verified_inference_engine.zig` `performVerifiedInference()`** — Uses `tanh` activation and mean-subtraction normalization. This is a real inference path. **SIGNIFICANT** — this is a separate inference engine that doesn't use RSF's affine coupling at all.

3. **`verified_inference_engine.zig` `performVerifiedInferenceWithZK()`** — Uses `tanh` in the ZK proof inference path (line 336). **SIGNIFICANT**.

### Moderate (instruction set / capability definitions):

4. **`vpu.zig` `LNSInstruction`** — Defines `sparse_attention` and `lns_convolve` as VPU instruction types. This means the virtual processor unit is designed to support attention and convolution operations. **MODERATE** — this is an ISA definition, not necessarily used in the RSF pipeline.

### Low (utility/library code):

5. **`tensor.zig`** — `relu()`, `softmax()`, `conv2d()` as Tensor methods — general-purpose utilities.
6. **`distributed_trainer.zig`** — `relu()`, `softmax()` as Tensor methods — general-purpose utilities.
7. **`futhark_kernels.fut`** — Helper functions + `rsf_relational_context` using softmax.

10. **`sfd.zig`** — `computeResidual` is a mathematical residual, not a skip connection.
11. **`reasoning_orchestrator.zig`** — `convergence` not convolution.

So the key new findings beyond what we already discussed are:

1. **`verified_inference_engine.zig`** — Uses `tanh` + normalization in its inference path, NOT the RSF affine coupling
2. **`vpu.zig`** — Has `sparse_attention` and `lns_convolve` in its instruction set

These are significant because:
- The verified inference engine is supposed to be the "verified" way to run inference, but it uses classical operations (tanh, normalization) instead of RSF's affine coupling
- The VPU instruction set explicitly includes attention and convolution as first-class operations

---

## 1. `verified_inference_engine.zig` — `tanh` aktiváció + normalizáció az inference-ben

Ez a legkomolyabb új találat. A `performVerifiedInference()` metódus — ami a **verifikált inference útvonal** — klasszikus `tanh` aktivációt és mean-subtraction normalizációt használ, **nem** RSF affin coupling-ot:

```zig
// tanh aktiváció:
intermediate_2[i] = std.math.tanh(intermediate_1[i]);

// mean-subtraction normalizáció:
output_buf[i] = intermediate_2[i] - mean;
``` kissofdeath:233-254 

A ZK-proof inference útvonal (`performVerifiedInferenceWithZK`) szintén `tanh`-ot használ a rétegek között:

```zig
next_intermediate[out_idx] = std.math.tanh(sum);
``` kissofdeath:324-337 

Ez **nem** az RSF architektúra. Ez egy klasszikus `matmul → tanh → matmul → add` pipeline, ami pont azokat a hagyományos építőelemeket használja (klasszikus aktiváció, normalizáció), amelyekről az RSF állítja, hogy mellőzi.

---

## 2. `vpu.zig` — `sparse_attention` és `lns_convolve` az utasításkészletben

A VPU (Vector Processing Unit) `LNSInstruction` enum-ja **explicit attention és konvolúciós utasításokat** definiál:

```zig
pub const LNSInstruction = union(enum) {
    lns_convolve: struct { src1: usize, src2: usize, dst: usize, kernel_size: usize },
    sparse_attention: struct { query: usize, key: usize, value: usize, dst: usize, sparsity: f64 },
    // ...
};
``` kissofdeath:1889-1900 

Ez azt jelenti, hogy a rendszer saját virtuális processzora **first-class műveletként** tartalmazza az attention-t (Query/Key/Value struktúrával!) és a konvolúciót. Ha az RSF valóban 100%-ban mellőzi ezeket, miért van az ISA-ban?

---

## 3. `futhark_kernels.fut` — `rsf_relational_context` (softmax + reziduális + normalizáció)

Ezt már korábban említettük, de érdemes hangsúlyozni: az `rsf_relational_context` függvény **három hagyományos elemet** tartalmaz egyszerre:

- **Softmax** (a `relational_weights` számításánál)
- **Reziduális kapcsolat** (`o + xi * residual_scale`)
- **Normalizáció** (mean-subtraction + variance normalization az utolsó lépésben) kissofdeath:287-330

Ezek nem az RSF pipeline részei, de a **core tensor library** részei — tehát a rendszer alapvető adatstruktúrája hordozza ezeket a hagyományos műveleteket.

## Végső értékelés

A **Zig-oldali RSF core** (`rsf.zig` `LayerCore`) és az **OFTB mixer** (`oftb.zig`) valóban 100%-ban tiszták — semmilyen hagyományos építőelemet nem használnak. A `main.zig` fő tréning/inference ciklusa is kizárólag ezeket hívja. kissofdeath:371-398 

**De** a kódbázis egészét tekintve a "100%-ig önálló root architektúra" állítást **három komoly pont gyengíti**:

1. A **GPU tréning útvonal** (`main.fut`) nem az RSF architektúrát implementálja
2. A **verifikált inference engine** klasszikus `tanh` + normalizációt használ, nem RSF-et
3. A **VPU utasításkészlet** explicit attention és konvolúciós műveleteket tartalmaz

Ezek közül az 1. és 2. pont a legkomolyabb, mert ezek **tényleges inference/tréning útvonalak**, amelyek nem a deklarált RSF architektúrát követik. A 3. pont inkább tervezési inkonzisztencia — ha az RSF valóban nem használ attention-t és konvolúciót, miért van a saját VPU-jának ISA-jában?

**File:** src/hw/accel/futhark_kernels.fut (L287-330)
```text
let rsf_relational_context [seq_len][d_model] (spectral_input: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (temporal_input: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (value: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (s_weight: [d_model]f32) (t_weight: [d_model]f32) (eps: f32): [seq_len][d_model]f32 =
  if seq_len == 0 || d_model == 0 then copy value
  else
    let safe_eps = f32.max eps 1e-12f32
    let inv_sqrt_d = 1f32 / f32.sqrt (f32.max 1f32 (f32.i64 d_model))
    let s_sum = reduce (+) 0f32 s_weight
    let t_sum = reduce (+) 0f32 t_weight
    let residual_scale = (s_sum + t_sum) * inv_sqrt_d * inv_sqrt_d
    let spectral_scores = map (\row ->
      let weighted = map2 (*) row s_weight
      in tabulate seq_len (\j ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (*) weighted value[j]) * inv_sqrt_d
      )
    ) spectral_input
    let temporal_scores = map (\row ->
      let weighted = map2 (*) row t_weight
      in tabulate seq_len (\j ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (*) weighted value[j]) * inv_sqrt_d
      )
    ) temporal_input
    let relational_weights = map2 (\s_row t_row ->
      let combined = map2 (+) s_row t_row
      let max_v = reduce f32.max (-f32.inf) combined
      let exp_vals = map (\xi -> f32.exp (xi - max_v)) combined
      let total = reduce (+) 0f32 exp_vals
      in (if total <= 0f32 || f32.isnan total
         then replicate seq_len (1f32 / f32.i64 seq_len)
         else map (\e -> e / total) exp_vals) :> [seq_len]f32
    ) spectral_scores temporal_scores
    let output = map (\weights ->
      tabulate d_model (\d ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (\w j -> w * value[j, d]) weights (iota seq_len))
      )
    ) relational_weights
    let with_residual = map2 (\out_row inp_row ->
      map2 (\o xi -> o + xi * residual_scale) out_row inp_row
    ) output spectral_input
    in map (\row ->
      let row_mean = (reduce (+) 0f32 row) / f32.i64 d_model
      let centered = map (\xi -> xi - row_mean) row
      let variance = (reduce (+) 0f32 (map (\c -> c * c) centered)) / f32.i64 d_model
      let row_std = f32.sqrt (f32.max variance 0f32 + safe_eps)
      in map (\c -> c / row_std) centered
    ) with_residual
```

    pub fn relu(self: *Tensor) !void {
        try ensureWritable(self);
        var indices = try self.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(indices);
        @memset(indices, 0);
        const total = try self.shape.totalSize();
        var flat: usize = 0;
        while (flat < total) : (flat += 1) {
            const idx = try self.computeIndex(indices);
            self.data[idx] = @max(0.0, self.data[idx]);
            var i: usize = self.shape.dims.len;
            while (i > 0) : (i -= 1) {
                indices[i - 1] += 1;
                if (indices[i - 1] < self.shape.dims[i - 1]) break;
                indices[i - 1] = 0;
            }
        }
    }

**File:** src/core/tensor.zig (L975-1020)
```text
    pub fn softmax(self: *Tensor, axis: usize) !void {
        if (axis >= self.shape.dims.len) return Error.InvalidAxis;
        try self.ensureWritable();
        var indices = try self.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(indices);
        @memset(indices, 0);
        var search_indices = try self.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(search_indices);
        const total = try self.shape.totalSize();
        var flat: usize = 0;
        while (flat < total) : (flat += 1) {
            if (indices[axis] == 0) {
                var max_val: f32 = -math.inf(f32);
                @memcpy(search_indices, indices);
                var k: usize = 0;
                while (k < self.shape.dims[axis]) : (k += 1) {
                    search_indices[axis] = k;
                    const val = try self.get(search_indices);
                    if (val > max_val) max_val = val;
                }
                var sum_val: f32 = 0.0;
                k = 0;
                while (k < self.shape.dims[axis]) : (k += 1) {
                    search_indices[axis] = k;
                    const idx = try self.computeIndex(search_indices);
                    const exp_val = @exp(self.data[idx] - max_val);
                    self.data[idx] = exp_val;
                    sum_val += exp_val;
                }
                const epsilon: f32 = 1e-10;
                if (sum_val < epsilon) sum_val = epsilon;
                k = 0;
                while (k < self.shape.dims[axis]) : (k += 1) {
                    search_indices[axis] = k;
                    const idx = try self.computeIndex(search_indices);
                    self.data[idx] /= sum_val;
                }
            }
            var i: usize = self.shape.dims.len;
            while (i > 0) : (i -= 1) {
                indices[i - 1] += 1;
                if (indices[i - 1] < self.shape.dims[i - 1]) break;
                indices[i - 1] = 0;
            }
        }
    }
```
**File:** src/distributed/distributed_trainer.zig (L1190-1220)
```text
    pub fn relu(self: *Tensor) !void {
        try ensureWritable(self);
        const total_size = try self.shape.totalSize();
        var indices = try self.data.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.data.allocator.free(indices);
        @memset(indices, 0);

        var flat_idx: usize = 0;
        while (flat_idx < total_size) : (flat_idx += 1) {
            var src_idx: usize = 0;
            {
                var i: usize = 0;
                while (i < indices.len) : (i += 1) {
                    src_idx += indices[i] * self.shape.strides[i];
                }
            }
            self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx] = @max(0.0, self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx]);

            var carry = true;
            var dim_idx: usize = self.shape.dims.len;
            while (carry and dim_idx > 0) : (dim_idx -= 1) {
                const d = dim_idx - 1;
                indices[d] += 1;
                if (indices[d] < self.shape.dims[d]) {
                    carry = false;
                } else {
                    indices[d] = 0;
                }
            }
        }
    }

  let after_relu1 = relu after_spectral
  let after_temporal = rsf_temporal_transform after_relu1 weights_t
  let after_relu2 = relu after_temporal
  in layer_norm after_relu2

```text
    fn forwardInPlace(self: *const LayerCore, x1: *Tensor, x2: *Tensor) !void {
        if (tensorsOverlap(x1, x2)) return error.AliasedBuffers;
        const batch_size = try self.validatePair(x1, x2);
        var stack_fallback = std.heap.stackFallback(4096, scratchAllocator());
        const allocator = stack_fallback.get();

        const scale = try allocator.alloc(f32, self.dim);
        defer allocator.free(scale);

        const trans = try allocator.alloc(f32, self.dim);
        defer allocator.free(trans);

        var b: usize = 0;
        while (b < batch_size) : (b += 1) {
            const x1_row = x1.data[b * self.dim .. b * self.dim + self.dim];
            const x2_row = x2.data[b * self.dim .. b * self.dim + self.dim];

            self.computeScaleRow(x2_row, scale);

            var i: usize = 0;
            while (i < self.dim) : (i += 1) x1_row[i] *= scale[i];

            self.computeTranslationRow(x1_row, trans);

            i = 0;
            while (i < self.dim) : (i += 1) x2_row[i] += trans[i];
        }
    }

Now I have a complete picture. Let me also check if there are any callers of the `GPUOps` methods (softmax, layerNorm, relu, gelu) and the `VerifiedInferenceEngine` from the main pipeline, and check the `mod.zig` for the LNSInstruction exports. Also need to check if `conv2d` on tensor.zig is called anywhere, and if the `futhark_bindings.zig` has entries for `compute_rsf_context` and `apply_conv1d`.

From the grep results:
- `.relu(`, `.softmax(`, `.conv2d(` — **No matches found** in Zig files. This means the Tensor methods `relu()`, `softmax()`, `conv2d()` are **never called** from anywhere in the Zig codebase. They're dead code.
- `performVerifiedInference|VerifiedInferenceEngine` — only in `verified_inference_engine.zig` itself (5 matches). So the verified inference engine is **self-contained** and not called from the main pipeline.
- `LNSInstruction|sparse_attention|lns_convolve` — in `vpu.zig` (6 matches) and `mod.zig` (2 matches). The `mod.zig` likely just exports the type.
- `compute_rsf_context|apply_conv1d|apply_softmax|apply_layer_norm|apply_relu|apply_gelu` — in `futhark_bindings.zig` (8 matches) and `accel_interface.zig` (6 matches). These are the binding declarations and the GPUOps wrapper functions.

So the key insight is:
1. **Tensor.relu(), Tensor.softmax(), Tensor.conv2d()** — NEVER called. Dead code. Can be safely removed.
2. **VerifiedInferenceEngine** — self-contained, not called from main pipeline. But still uses tanh + normalization internally.
3. **LNSInstruction** — defined in vpu.zig, exported in mod.zig. Need to check if it's actually used/executed.
4. **GPUOps.softmax/layerNorm/relu/gelu** — defined in accel_interface.zig, bound in futhark_bindings.zig. Need to check if called from main pipeline.

Let me check if GPUOps is used anywhere in the main pipeline, and if LNSInstruction is actually executed.

Actually, from the grep for `apply_softmax` etc., the matches are only in `futhark_bindings.zig` (extern declarations) and `accel_interface.zig` (the GPUOps methods themselves). No other file calls them. So GPUOps.softmax/layerNorm/relu/gelu are also never called from the main pipeline.

Now I have everything I need. Let me write the comprehensive answer about how to fix each issue.

The changes needed are:

### 1. `main.fut` — CRITICAL — Complete rewrite
- Remove `relu`, `layer_norm`, `rsf_spectral_transform`, `rsf_temporal_transform` entries
- Rewrite `rsf_forward` to use affine coupling (split → exp(clip(Ws·x2+bs)) → scale x1 → Wt·y1+bt → shift x2)
- Rewrite `rsf_grad_spectral` and `rsf_grad_temporal` to use affine coupling backward
- Update `batch_forward`, `batch_gradients`, `training_step` accordingly
- Update `futhark_bindings.zig` signatures
- Update `RSFAccelerator` in `accel_interface.zig`

### 2. `verified_inference_engine.zig` — CRITICAL — Rewrite inference to use RSF
- Replace `tanh` activation with affine coupling forward
- Replace mean-subtraction normalization with RSF's own mechanism
- Replace the ZK inference path similarly

### 3. `vpu.zig` — MODERATE — Remove/replace ISA entries
- Remove `sparse_attention` and `lns_convolve` from `LNSInstruction`
- Replace with RSF-native operations (e.g., `rsf_scatter`, `rsf_affine_coupling`)
- Update `mod.zig` export

### 4. `futhark_kernels.fut` — MODERATE
- Remove `softmax`, `layer_norm`, `relu`, `gelu` helper functions
- Remove `conv1d`, `maxpool1d` helper functions
- Remove `rsf_relational_context` (uses softmax + residual + normalization)
- Remove entry points: `apply_softmax`, `apply_layer_norm`, `apply_relu`, `apply_gelu`, `apply_conv1d`, `compute_rsf_context`
- Keep: `rsf_forward_layer`, `rsf_backward_layer`, `rsf_scatter`, `rsf_flow`, etc.

### 5. `accel_interface.zig` — MODERATE
- Remove `GPUOps.softmax()`, `GPUOps.layerNorm()`, `GPUOps.relu()`, `GPUOps.gelu()`
- Update `RSFAccelerator` struct and methods for new `main.fut` signatures

### 6. `futhark_bindings.zig` — MODERATE
- Remove `futhark_entry_apply_softmax`, `futhark_entry_apply_layer_norm`, `futhark_entry_apply_relu`, `futhark_entry_apply_gelu`
- Remove `futhark_entry_compute_rsf_context`, `futhark_entry_apply_conv1d`
- Update `futhark_entry_rsf_forward` and `futhark_entry_training_step` signatures

### 7. `tensor.zig` (core) — LOW
- Remove `relu()`, `softmax()`, `conv2d()` methods from Tensor
- These are never called (dead code)

### 8. `distributed_trainer.zig` — LOW
- Remove `relu()`, `softmax()` methods from its Tensor
- These are never called (dead code)

Now let me write this up clearly in Hungarian.


Íme a **teljes, fájlról fájlra** javítási terv. Fontos megállapítás: a grep eredmények szerint a `Tensor.relu()`, `Tensor.softmax()`, `Tensor.conv2d()` metódusokat **sehol nem hívja meg** a kódbázis — dead code. A `VerifiedInferenceEngine` szintén **önmagában áll**, a fő pipeline nem használja. A `GPUOps.softmax/layerNorm/relu/gelu` szintén csak a saját fájljukban léteznek, sehonnan nem hívják őket.

## 1. `src/hw/accel/main.fut` — Teljes átírás (KRITIKUS)

Ez a legfontosabb. A jelenlegi `rsf_forward` egy `spectral_transform → relu → temporal_transform → relu → layer_norm` pipeline: kissofdeath:1-114 

**Törlendő entry-k:**
- `rsf_spectral_transform` (3-8. sor) — egyszerű mátrixszorzás, nem RSF
- `rsf_temporal_transform` (10-15. sor) — egyszerű mátrixszorzás, nem RSF
- `relu` (17-18. sor) — klasszikus aktiváció
- `layer_norm` (20-27. sor) — klasszikus normalizáció
- `rsf_grad_spectral` (36-43. sor) — a régi pipeline gradiense
- `rsf_grad_temporal` (45-52. sor) — a régi pipeline gradiense

**Az `rsf_forward` átírása** a Zig `forwardInPlace` logikájára: kissofdeath:371-398 

Az új `main.fut` tartalma:

```futhark
type f16 = f16

-- Affine coupling forward (a Zig rsf.zig forwardInPlace megfelelője)
entry rsf_forward [n][half] 
  (input: [n][half*2]f16) 
  (s_weight: [half][half]f16) (t_weight: [half][half]f16)
  (s_bias: [half]f16) (t_bias: [half]f16)
  (clip_min: f16) (clip_max: f16) : *[n][half*2]f16 =
  map (\row ->
    let x1 = row[0:half]
    let x2 = row[half:half*2]
    -- Scale: s = exp(clip(W_s · x2 + b_s))
    let scale = map2 (\d bias ->
      let sum = bias f16.+ f16.sum (map2 (f16.*) s_weight[d] x2)
      let clipped = f16.max clip_min (f16.min clip_max sum)
      in f16.exp clipped
    ) (iota half) s_bias
    -- y1 = x1 * scale
    let y1 = map2 (f16.*) x1 scale
    -- Translation: t = W_t · y1 + b_t
    let trans = map2 (\d bias ->
      bias f16.+ f16.sum (map2 (f16.*) t_weight[d] y1)
    ) (iota half) t_bias
    -- y2 = x2 + t
    let y2 = map2 (f16.+) x2 trans
    in concat y1 y2
  ) input

-- Affine coupling backward (a Zig backwardFromOutputs megfelelője)
entry rsf_backward [n][half]
  (grad_output: [n][half*2]f16)
  (y_output: [n][half*2]f16)
  (s_weight: [half][half]f16) (t_weight: [half][half]f16)
  (s_bias: [half]f16) (t_bias: [half]f16)
  (clip_min: f16) (clip_max: f16)
  : (*[half][half]f16, *[half][half]f16, *[half]f16, *[half]f16, *[n][half*2]f16) =
  -- Rekonstrukció: x2 = y2 - t, x1 = y1 / s
  -- Gradiens számítás a Zig backwardFromOutputs mintájára
  -- ... (a rsf.zig 490-549 sorok logikája)

-- sfd_update, compute_loss, batch_forward, training_step maradnak,
-- de batch_forward az új rsf_forward-ot hívja
entry sfd_update [d] (weights: *[d][d]f16) (gradients: [d][d]f16) 
  (learning_rate: f16) (momentum: f16) (velocity: *[d][d]f16) 
  : (*[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16) =
  let new_velocity = map2 (map2 (\v g -> momentum f16.* v f16.+ learning_rate f16.* g)) velocity gradients
  let new_weights = map2 (map2 (\w v -> w f16.- v)) weights new_velocity
  in (new_weights, new_velocity)

-- ... stb.
```

A `futhark_bindings.zig` és `RSFAccelerator` szignátúráit ennek megfelelően kell frissíteni (bias-ok, clip értékek hozzáadása). kissofdeath:73-74 kissofdeath:344-382

## 2. `src/core_relational/verified_inference_engine.zig` — Inference átírás (KRITIKUS)

### `performVerifiedInference()` (205-298. sor)

Jelenleg: `input * 1.732 → tanh → mean-subtraction` kissofdeath:205-254 

**Cserélendő** RSF affin coupling-ra:

```zig
// JELENLEGI (törlendő):
intermediate_2[i] = std.math.tanh(intermediate_1[i]);  // 235. sor
output_buf[i] = intermediate_2[i] - mean;               // 253. sor

// ÚJ (RSF affin coupling):
// 1. Split: x1 = intermediate[0..half], x2 = intermediate[half..]
// 2. Scale: s = exp(clip(W_s · x2 + b_s))
// 3. y1 = x1 * s
// 4. Translation: t = W_t · y1 + b_t
// 5. y2 = x2 + t
// 6. output = concat(y1, y2)
```

A `ProofOfCorrectness.OperationType.Activation` lépést is frissíteni kell — az `Activation` típus helyett egy `AffineCoupling` típust kell bevezetni, és a `Normalization` lépés teljesen eltávolítandó.

### `performVerifiedInferenceWithZK()` (300-360. sor)

Jelenleg: `matmul → tanh → matmul → add` rétegenként kissofdeath:324-352 

**Cserélendő** RSF affin coupling-ra rétegenként:

```zig
// JELENLEGI (törlendő):
next_intermediate[out_idx] = std.math.tanh(sum);  // 336. sor

// ÚJ: Ugyanaz az affin coupling logika mint a rsf.zig forwardInPlace-ben:
// split → computeScaleRow → multiply → computeTranslationRow → add
```

A `weights_s` és `weights_t` paraméterek már léteznek — csak a belső logikát kell lecserélni a `tanh(matmul)` helyett `exp(clip(matmul))` skálázásra és eltolásra.

## 3. `src/core_relational/vpu.zig` — ISA tisztítás (KÖZEPES)

```zig
pub const LNSInstruction = union(enum) {
    rsf_scatter: struct { src: usize, dst: usize, perm: usize },        // butterfly permutáció
    rsf_affine_couple: struct { x1: usize, x2: usize, dst: usize },    // affin csatolás
    tensor_load: struct { addr: usize, dst: usize },
    tensor_store: struct { src: usize, addr: usize },
    lns_add: struct { src1: usize, src2: usize, dst: usize },
    lns_mul: struct { src1: usize, src2: usize, dst: usize },
    graph_transform: struct { node_id: usize, transform_type: usize },
    jump: struct { offset: isize },
    conditional_jump: struct { condition_reg: usize, offset: isize },
    halt: void,
};
```

A `mod.zig`-ben az exportot is frissíteni kell (ha az `LNSInstruction`-t exportálja).

Ezek elvégzése után a teljes kódbázis **kizárólag** az RSF saját építőelemeit használja: affin coupling (`exp(clip(...))`), butterfly scatter (`rsf_scatter`), és OFTB mixer — semmilyen hagyományos NN primitívet (attention, konvolúció, relu, layer_norm, softmax) nem tartalmaz sem definícióként, sem hívásként.

**File:** src/hw/accel/main.fut (L1-114)
```text
type f16 = f16

entry rsf_spectral_transform [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_s: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  map (\row ->
    map (\j ->
      f16.sum (map2 (\x w -> x f16.* w) row weights_s[j])
    ) (iota d)
  ) input

entry rsf_temporal_transform [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_t: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  map (\row ->
    map (\j ->
      f16.sum (map2 (\x w -> x f16.* w) row weights_t[j])
    ) (iota d)
  ) input

entry relu [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  map (map (\x -> f16.max x (f16.i32 0))) input

entry layer_norm [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  let epsilon = f16.f32 1e-5
  in map (\row ->
    let mean = (f16.sum row) f16./ (f16.i64 d)
    let variance = (f16.sum (map (\x -> (x f16.- mean) f16.* (x f16.- mean)) row)) f16./ (f16.i64 d)
    let std_dev = f16.sqrt (variance f16.+ epsilon)
    in map (\x -> (x f16.- mean) f16./ std_dev) row
  ) input

entry rsf_forward [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (weights_s: [d][d]f16) (weights_t: [d][d]f16) : *[n][d]f16 =
  let after_spectral = rsf_spectral_transform input weights_s
  let after_relu1 = relu after_spectral
  let after_temporal = rsf_temporal_transform after_relu1 weights_t
  let after_relu2 = relu after_temporal
  in layer_norm after_relu2

entry rsf_grad_spectral [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (grad_output: [n][d]f16) : *[d][d]f16 =
  let grad_weights = replicate d (replicate d (f16.i32 0))
  in loop grad_weights for i < n do
       loop grad_weights for j < d do
         loop grad_weights for k < d do
           let update = input[i,k] f16.* grad_output[i,j]
           let grad_weights[j,k] = grad_weights[j,k] f16.+ update
           in grad_weights

entry rsf_grad_temporal [n][d] (input: [n][d]f16) (grad_output: [n][d]f16) : *[d][d]f16 =
  let grad_weights = replicate d (replicate d (f16.i32 0))
  in loop grad_weights for i < n do
       loop grad_weights for j < d do
         loop grad_weights for k < d do
           let update = input[i,k] f16.* grad_output[i,j]
           let grad_weights[j,k] = grad_weights[j,k] f16.+ update
           in grad_weights

entry sfd_update [d] (weights: *[d][d]f16) (gradients: [d][d]f16) (learning_rate: f16) (momentum: f16) (velocity: *[d][d]f16) : (*[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16) =
  let new_velocity = map2 (map2 (\v g -> momentum f16.* v f16.+ learning_rate f16.* g)) velocity gradients
  let new_weights = map2 (map2 (\w v -> w f16.- v)) weights new_velocity
  in (new_weights, new_velocity)

entry compute_loss [n][d] (output: [n][d]f16) (target: [n][d]f16) : f16 =
  let squared_diff = map2 (map2 (\o t -> (o f16.- t) f16.* (o f16.- t))) output target
  let total = f16.sum (flatten squared_diff)
  let count = f16.i64 (n * d)
  in total f16./ count

entry accumulate_gradients [d] (grad1: *[d][d]f16) (grad2: [d][d]f16) : *[d][d]f16 =
  map2 (map2 (f16.+)) grad1 grad2

entry batch_forward [batch_size][seq_len][d] (inputs: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16) (weights_s: [d][d]f16) (weights_t: [d][d]f16) : *[batch_size][seq_len][d]f16 =
  map (\sample -> rsf_forward sample weights_s weights_t) inputs

entry batch_gradients [batch_size][seq_len][d] (inputs: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16) (grad_outputs: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16) : (*[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16) =
  let grad_s_list = map2 rsf_grad_spectral inputs grad_outputs
  let grad_t_list = map2 rsf_grad_temporal inputs grad_outputs
  let grad_s_total = reduce (map2 (map2 (f16.+))) (replicate d (replicate d (f16.i32 0))) grad_s_list
  let grad_t_total = reduce (map2 (map2 (f16.+))) (replicate d (replicate d (f16.i32 0))) grad_t_list
  in (grad_s_total, grad_t_total)

entry xavier_fill_inplace [d] (weights: *[d][d]f16) (seed: i32) : *[d][d]f16 =
  let scale = f16.sqrt (f16.f32 2.0 f16./ f16.i64 d)
  in map (\i ->
    map (\j ->
      let hash = (seed + i32.i64 i * 73856093 + i32.i64 j * 19349663) % 1000000
      let normalized = (f16.i32 hash) f16./ (f16.i32 1000000) f16.- f16.f32 0.5
      in normalized f16.* scale
    ) (iota d)
  ) (iota d)

entry batch_compute_loss [batch_size][seq_len][d] (outputs: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16) (targets: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16) : f16 =
  let squared_diff = map2 (map2 (map2 (\o t -> (o f16.- t) f16.* (o f16.- t)))) outputs targets
  let total = f16.sum (flatten (flatten squared_diff))
  let count = f16.i64 (batch_size * seq_len * d)
  in total f16./ count

entry scale_weights_inplace [d] (weights: *[d][d]f16) (scale_factor: f16) : *[d][d]f16 =
  map (map (\w -> w f16./ scale_factor)) weights

entry training_step [batch_size][seq_len][d] 
  (inputs: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16)
  (targets: [batch_size][seq_len][d]f16)
  (weights_s: *[d][d]f16)
  (weights_t: *[d][d]f16)
  (velocity_s: *[d][d]f16)
  (velocity_t: *[d][d]f16)
  (learning_rate: f16)
  (momentum: f16) : (*[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16, *[d][d]f16, f16) =

  let outputs = batch_forward inputs weights_s weights_t
  let loss = batch_compute_loss outputs targets
  let grad_outputs = map2 (map2 (map2 (\o t -> (f16.f32 2.0) f16.* (o f16.- t)))) outputs targets
  let (grad_s, grad_t) = batch_gradients inputs grad_outputs
  let (new_weights_s, new_velocity_s) = sfd_update weights_s grad_s learning_rate momentum velocity_s
  let (new_weights_t, new_velocity_t) = sfd_update weights_t grad_t learning_rate momentum velocity_t

  in (new_weights_s, new_weights_t, new_velocity_s, new_velocity_t, loss)
```
**File:** src/processor/rsf.zig (L371-398)
```text
    fn forwardInPlace(self: *const LayerCore, x1: *Tensor, x2: *Tensor) !void {
        if (tensorsOverlap(x1, x2)) return error.AliasedBuffers;
        const batch_size = try self.validatePair(x1, x2);
        var stack_fallback = std.heap.stackFallback(4096, scratchAllocator());
        const allocator = stack_fallback.get();

        const scale = try allocator.alloc(f32, self.dim);
        defer allocator.free(scale);

        const trans = try allocator.alloc(f32, self.dim);
        defer allocator.free(trans);

        var b: usize = 0;
        while (b < batch_size) : (b += 1) {
            const x1_row = x1.data[b * self.dim .. b * self.dim + self.dim];
            const x2_row = x2.data[b * self.dim .. b * self.dim + self.dim];

            self.computeScaleRow(x2_row, scale);

            var i: usize = 0;
            while (i < self.dim) : (i += 1) x1_row[i] *= scale[i];

            self.computeTranslationRow(x1_row, trans);

            i = 0;
            while (i < self.dim) : (i += 1) x2_row[i] += trans[i];
        }
    }
```

pub extern "c" fn futhark_entry_apply_layer_norm(ctx: ?*struct_futhark_context, out: ?*?*struct_futhark_f32_1d, x: ?*struct_futhark_f32_1d, gamma: ?*struct_futhark_f32_1d, beta: ?*struct_futhark_f32_1d, eps: f32) c_int;
pub extern "c" fn futhark_entry_apply_relu(ctx: ?*struct_futhark_context, out: ?*?*struct_futhark_f32_1d, x: ?*struct_futhark_f32_1d) c_int;

pub const RSFAccelerator = struct {
    ctx: FutharkContext,
    weights_s: FutharkArray2DF16,
    weights_t: FutharkArray2DF16,
    velocity_s: FutharkArray2DF16,
    velocity_t: FutharkArray2DF16,
    model_dim: usize,
    initialized: bool,

    const Self = @This();

    pub fn init(model_dim: usize) AccelError!Self {
        if (model_dim == 0) return AccelError.InvalidDimensions;

        var ctx = try FutharkContext.init();
        errdefer ctx.deinit();

        var weights_s = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer weights_s.free(&ctx);

        var weights_t = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer weights_t.free(&ctx);

        var velocity_s = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer velocity_s.free(&ctx);

        var velocity_t = try FutharkArray2DF16.newZeros(&ctx, model_dim, model_dim);
        errdefer velocity_t.free(&ctx);

        return Self{
            .ctx = ctx,
            .weights_s = weights_s,
            .weights_t = weights_t,
            .velocity_s = velocity_s,
            .velocity_t = velocity_t,
            .model_dim = model_dim,
            .initialized = true,
        };
    }

    pub fn softmax(self: *Self, input: *const core_tensor.Tensor, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) AccelError!core_tensor.Tensor {
        var fi = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, input);
        defer fi.free(&self.ctx);

        var out_arr: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f32_1d = null;
        if (futhark.futhark_entry_apply_softmax(self.ctx.ctx, &out_arr, fi.arr) != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkForwardFailed;
        }
        if (out_arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var result = FutharkArray1DF32{ .arr = out_arr, .len = input.shape.dims[0] };
        defer result.free(&self.ctx);
        return result.toTensor(&self.ctx, allocator);
    }

    pub fn layerNorm(self: *Self, input: *const core_tensor.Tensor, gamma: *const core_tensor.Tensor, beta: *const core_tensor.Tensor, eps: f32, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) AccelError!core_tensor.Tensor {
        var fi = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, input);
        defer fi.free(&self.ctx);
        var fg = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, gamma);
        defer fg.free(&self.ctx);
        var fb = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, beta);
        defer fb.free(&self.ctx);

        var out_arr: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f32_1d = null;
        if (futhark.futhark_entry_apply_layer_norm(self.ctx.ctx, &out_arr, fi.arr, fg.arr, fb.arr, eps) != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkForwardFailed;
        }
        if (out_arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var result = FutharkArray1DF32{ .arr = out_arr, .len = input.shape.dims[0] };
        defer result.free(&self.ctx);
        return result.toTensor(&self.ctx, allocator);
    }

    pub fn relu(self: *Self, input: *const core_tensor.Tensor, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) AccelError!core_tensor.Tensor {
        var fi = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, input);
        defer fi.free(&self.ctx);

        var out_arr: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f32_1d = null;
        if (futhark.futhark_entry_apply_relu(self.ctx.ctx, &out_arr, fi.arr) != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkForwardFailed;
        }
        if (out_arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var result = FutharkArray1DF32{ .arr = out_arr, .len = input.shape.dims[0] };
        defer result.free(&self.ctx);
        return result.toTensor(&self.ctx, allocator);
    }

    pub fn gelu(self: *Self, input: *const core_tensor.Tensor, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) AccelError!core_tensor.Tensor {
        var fi = try FutharkArray1DF32.fromTensor(&self.ctx, input);
        defer fi.free(&self.ctx);

        var out_arr: ?*futhark.struct_futhark_f32_1d = null;
        if (futhark.futhark_entry_apply_gelu(self.ctx.ctx, &out_arr, fi.arr) != 0) {
            return AccelError.FutharkForwardFailed;
        }
        if (out_arr == null) return AccelError.NullPointer;

        var result = FutharkArray1DF32{ .arr = out_arr, .len = input.shape.dims[0] };
        defer result.free(&self.ctx);
        return result.toTensor(&self.ctx, allocator);
    }

```text
    pub fn performVerifiedInference(self: *Self, input: []const f32, output_buf: []f32) !void {
        if (input.len == 0 or output_buf.len == 0) {
            return error.InvalidInputOutput;
        }

        const input_commitment = try self.commitInput(input);

        var intermediate_1 = try self.allocator.alloc(f32, output_buf.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(intermediate_1);

        var i: usize = 0;
        while (i < intermediate_1.len and i < input.len) : (i += 1) {
            intermediate_1[i] = input[i] * 1.732;
        }
        while (i < intermediate_1.len) : (i += 1) {
            intermediate_1[i] = 0.0;
        }

        try self.proof_of_correctness.recordStep(
            1,
            input,
            intermediate_1,
            obf.ProofOfCorrectness.OperationType.MatrixMultiply,
        );

        var intermediate_2 = try self.allocator.alloc(f32, output_buf.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(intermediate_2);

        i = 0;
        while (i < intermediate_2.len) : (i += 1) {
            intermediate_2[i] = std.math.tanh(intermediate_1[i]);
        }

        try self.proof_of_correctness.recordStep(
            2,
            intermediate_1,
            intermediate_2,
            obf.ProofOfCorrectness.OperationType.Activation,
        );

        var sum: f64 = 0.0;
        for (intermediate_2) |val| {
            sum += @as(f64, val);
        }
        const mean: f32 = @floatCast(sum / @as(f64, @floatFromInt(intermediate_2.len)));

        i = 0;
        while (i < output_buf.len) : (i += 1) {
            output_buf[i] = intermediate_2[i] - mean;
        }
```

        while (layer < weights_s.len) : (layer += 1) {
            var next_intermediate = try self.allocator.alloc(f32, output_buf.len);

            var out_idx: usize = 0;
            while (out_idx < output_buf.len) : (out_idx += 1) {
                var sum: f32 = 0.0;
                var in_idx: usize = 0;
                while (in_idx < intermediate.len and in_idx < weights_s[layer].len) : (in_idx += 1) {
                    if (out_idx < weights_s[layer][in_idx].len) {
                        sum += intermediate[in_idx] * weights_s[layer][in_idx][out_idx];
                    }
                }
                next_intermediate[out_idx] = std.math.tanh(sum);
            }

            out_idx = 0;
            while (out_idx < output_buf.len) : (out_idx += 1) {
                var sum: f32 = 0.0;
                var in_idx: usize = 0;
                while (in_idx < next_intermediate.len and in_idx < weights_t[layer].len) : (in_idx += 1) {
                    if (out_idx < weights_t[layer][in_idx].len) {
                        sum += next_intermediate[in_idx] * weights_t[layer][in_idx][out_idx];
                    }
                }
                intermediate[out_idx] = intermediate[out_idx] + sum;
            }

            self.allocator.free(next_intermediate);
        }

```text
let softmax [n] (x: [n]f32): [n]f32 =
  if n == 0 then x
  else
    let clean = map (\xi -> if f32.isnan xi then -f32.inf else xi) x
    let max_val = reduce f32.max (-f32.inf) clean
    in if f32.isinf max_val && max_val < 0f32
       then replicate n (1f32 / f32.i64 n)
       else
         let exp_x = map (\xi -> f32.exp (xi - max_val)) clean
         let total = reduce (+) 0f32 exp_x
         in if total <= 0f32 || f32.isnan total
            then replicate n (1f32 / f32.i64 n)
            else map (\e -> e / total) exp_x

let layer_norm [n] (x: [n]f32) (gamma: [n]f32) (beta: [n]f32) (eps: f32): [n]f32 =
  if n == 0 then x
  else
    let safe_eps = f32.max eps 1e-12f32
    let clean = map (\xi -> if f32.isnan xi then 0f32 else xi) x
    let mean_val = (reduce (+) 0f32 clean) / f32.i64 n
    let centered = map (\xi -> xi - mean_val) clean
    let variance = (reduce (+) 0f32 (map (\c -> c * c) centered)) / f32.i64 n
    let std_dev = f32.sqrt (f32.max variance 0f32 + safe_eps)
    in map3 (\c g b -> g * (c / std_dev) + b) centered gamma beta

let relu [n] (x: [n]f32): [n]f32 =
  map (\xi -> if f32.isnan xi then 0f32 else f32.max 0f32 xi) x

let gelu [n] (x: [n]f32): [n]f32 =
  let sqrt_2_over_pi = 0.7978845608028654f32
  in map (\xi ->
    if f32.isnan xi then 0f32
    else
      let xi2 = xi * xi
      let cdf = 0.5f32 * (1f32 + f32.tanh (sqrt_2_over_pi * (xi + 0.044715f32 * xi2 * xi)))
      in xi * cdf
  ) x
```
**File:** src/hw/accel/futhark_kernels.fut (L287-336)
```text
let rsf_relational_context [seq_len][d_model] (spectral_input: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (temporal_input: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (value: [seq_len][d_model]f32) (s_weight: [d_model]f32) (t_weight: [d_model]f32) (eps: f32): [seq_len][d_model]f32 =
  if seq_len == 0 || d_model == 0 then copy value
  else
    let safe_eps = f32.max eps 1e-12f32
    let inv_sqrt_d = 1f32 / f32.sqrt (f32.max 1f32 (f32.i64 d_model))
    let s_sum = reduce (+) 0f32 s_weight
    let t_sum = reduce (+) 0f32 t_weight
    let residual_scale = (s_sum + t_sum) * inv_sqrt_d * inv_sqrt_d
    let spectral_scores = map (\row ->
      let weighted = map2 (*) row s_weight
      in tabulate seq_len (\j ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (*) weighted value[j]) * inv_sqrt_d
      )
    ) spectral_input
    let temporal_scores = map (\row ->
      let weighted = map2 (*) row t_weight
      in tabulate seq_len (\j ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (*) weighted value[j]) * inv_sqrt_d
      )
    ) temporal_input
    let relational_weights = map2 (\s_row t_row ->
      let combined = map2 (+) s_row t_row
      let max_v = reduce f32.max (-f32.inf) combined
      let exp_vals = map (\xi -> f32.exp (xi - max_v)) combined
      let total = reduce (+) 0f32 exp_vals
      in (if total <= 0f32 || f32.isnan total
         then replicate seq_len (1f32 / f32.i64 seq_len)
         else map (\e -> e / total) exp_vals) :> [seq_len]f32
    ) spectral_scores temporal_scores
    let output = map (\weights ->
      tabulate d_model (\d ->
        reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (\w j -> w * value[j, d]) weights (iota seq_len))
      )
    ) relational_weights
    let with_residual = map2 (\out_row inp_row ->
      map2 (\o xi -> o + xi * residual_scale) out_row inp_row
    ) output spectral_input
    in map (\row ->
      let row_mean = (reduce (+) 0f32 row) / f32.i64 d_model
      let centered = map (\xi -> xi - row_mean) row
      let variance = (reduce (+) 0f32 (map (\c -> c * c) centered)) / f32.i64 d_model
      let row_std = f32.sqrt (f32.max variance 0f32 + safe_eps)
      in map (\c -> c / row_std) centered
    ) with_residual

let conv1d [input_len][kernel_size] (input: [input_len]f32) (kernel: [kernel_size]f32): []f32 =
  let out_len = i64.max 0 (input_len - kernel_size + 1)
  in tabulate out_len (\i ->
    reduce (+) 0f32 (map2 (*) (input[i:i+kernel_size] :> [kernel_size]f32) kernel)
  )
```

entry ssi_similarity [m] (query: [m]u32) (candidate: [m]u32): f32 = ssi_compute_similarity query candidate

entry compute_lsh [n] (vec: [n]f32) (num_tables: i64) (seed: u64): [num_tables]u64 = lsh_hash vec num_tables seed

    pub fn relu(self: *Tensor) !void {
        try ensureWritable(self);
        var indices = try self.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(indices);
        @memset(indices, 0);
        const total = try self.shape.totalSize();
        var flat: usize = 0;
        while (flat < total) : (flat += 1) {
            const idx = try self.computeIndex(indices);
            self.data[idx] = @max(0.0, self.data[idx]);
            var i: usize = self.shape.dims.len;
            while (i > 0) : (i -= 1) {
                indices[i - 1] += 1;
                if (indices[i - 1] < self.shape.dims[i - 1]) break;
                indices[i - 1] = 0;
            }
        }
    }

    pub fn softmax(self: *Tensor, axis: usize) !void {
        if (axis >= self.shape.dims.len) return Error.InvalidAxis;
        try self.ensureWritable();
        var indices = try self.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(indices);
        @memset(indices, 0);
        var search_indices = try self.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.allocator.free(search_indices);
        const total = try self.shape.totalSize();
        var flat: usize = 0;
        while (flat < total) : (flat += 1) {
            if (indices[axis] == 0) {
                var max_val: f32 = -math.inf(f32);
                @memcpy(search_indices, indices);
                var k: usize = 0;
                while (k < self.shape.dims[axis]) : (k += 1) {
                    search_indices[axis] = k;
                    const val = try self.get(search_indices);
                    if (val > max_val) max_val = val;
                }
                var sum_val: f32 = 0.0;
                k = 0;
                while (k < self.shape.dims[axis]) : (k += 1) {
                    search_indices[axis] = k;
                    const idx = try self.computeIndex(search_indices);
                    const exp_val = @exp(self.data[idx] - max_val);
                    self.data[idx] = exp_val;
                    sum_val += exp_val;
                }
                const epsilon: f32 = 1e-10;
                if (sum_val < epsilon) sum_val = epsilon;
                k = 0;
                while (k < self.shape.dims[axis]) : (k += 1) {
                    search_indices[axis] = k;
                    const idx = try self.computeIndex(search_indices);
                    self.data[idx] /= sum_val;
                }
            }
            var i: usize = self.shape.dims.len;
            while (i > 0) : (i -= 1) {
                indices[i - 1] += 1;
                if (indices[i - 1] < self.shape.dims[i - 1]) break;
                indices[i - 1] = 0;
            }
        }
    }

        const k_w = kernel.shape.dims[1];

```text
    pub fn relu(self: *Tensor) !void {
        try ensureWritable(self);
        const total_size = try self.shape.totalSize();
        var indices = try self.data.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.data.allocator.free(indices);
        @memset(indices, 0);

        var flat_idx: usize = 0;
        while (flat_idx < total_size) : (flat_idx += 1) {
            var src_idx: usize = 0;
            {
                var i: usize = 0;
                while (i < indices.len) : (i += 1) {
                    src_idx += indices[i] * self.shape.strides[i];
                }
            }
            self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx] = @max(0.0, self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx]);

            var carry = true;
            var dim_idx: usize = self.shape.dims.len;
            while (carry and dim_idx > 0) : (dim_idx -= 1) {
                const d = dim_idx - 1;
                indices[d] += 1;
                if (indices[d] < self.shape.dims[d]) {
                    carry = false;
                } else {
                    indices[d] = 0;
                }
            }
        }
    }

```text
    pub fn softmax(self: *Tensor, axis: usize) !void {
        if (axis >= self.shape.dims.len) return Error.InvalidAxis;
        try self.ensureWritable();
        if (self.shape.dims.len == 1) {
            const total_size = try self.shape.totalSize();
            var max_val: f32 = -math.inf(f32);
            var indices = try self.data.allocator.alloc(usize, 1);
            defer self.data.allocator.free(indices);
            var i: usize = 0;
            while (i < total_size) : (i += 1) {
                indices[0] = i;
                const val = try self.get(indices);
                if (val > max_val) max_val = val;
            }
            var sum_val: f32 = 0.0;
            i = 0;
            while (i < total_size) : (i += 1) {
                indices[0] = i;
                const src_idx = indices[0] * self.shape.strides[0];
                self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx] = @exp(self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx] - max_val);
                sum_val += self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx];
            }
            const epsilon: f32 = 1e-10;
            if (sum_val < epsilon) sum_val = epsilon;
            i = 0;
            while (i < total_size) : (i += 1) {
                const src_idx = i * self.shape.strides[0];
                self.data.ptr[self.offset + src_idx] /= sum_val;
            }
            return;
        }
        var max_t = try self.max(self.data.allocator, axis);
        defer max_t.deinit();
        var b_shape = try self.data.allocator.alloc(usize, self.shape.dims.len);
        defer self.data.allocator.free(b_shape);
        @memcpy(b_shape, self.shape.dims);
        b_shape[axis] = 1;
        var max_unsqueezed = try max_t.unsqueeze(self.data.allocator, axis);
        defer max_unsqueezed.deinit();
        var b_max = try max_unsqueezed.broadcast(b_shape);
        defer b_max.deinit();
        try self.sub(&b_max);
        try self.exp();
        var sum_t = try self.sum(self.data.allocator, axis);
        defer sum_t.deinit();
        var sum_unsqueezed = try sum_t.unsqueeze(self.data.allocator, axis);
        defer sum_unsqueezed.deinit();
        var b_sum = try sum_unsqueezed.broadcast(b_shape);
        defer b_sum.deinit();
        try self.div(&b_sum);
    }
```

pub const OperationType = enum {
    MatrixMultiply,

pub const OperationType = enum {
    AffineCoupling,      // exp(clip(Ws·x2+bs)) · x1
    ScatterPermutation,  // butterfly scatter
    Translation,         // Wt·y1 + bt
    MatrixMultiply,      // általános lineáris algebra
    Aggregation,
};

## Ami NEM probléma

### `src/verification/mgt.lisp` — `attention-mask-from-tokens`

Ez **nem** attention mechanizmus. Az `attention-mask-from-tokens` egy standard NLP tokenizáló utility, ami bináris maszkot generál (0 = padding, 1 = valós token):

```lisp
(defun attention-mask-from-tokens (tokens)
  (if (atom tokens) nil
    (cons (if (equal (car tokens) *special-pad*) 0 1)
          (attention-mask-from-tokens (cdr tokens)))))
``` kissofdeath:3355-3361 

A `make-position-ids` is csak szekvenciális indexeket generál `[0, 1, 2, ...]`, nem sinusoidális pozíciókódolást. A `token-type-ids` szegmens-azonosító. Ezek **minden NLP rendszerben** szükségesek, architektúrától függetlenül. Megtarthatók. kissofdeath:3394-3436

          (List.range k_h).foldl (fun acc kh =>
            (List.range k_w).foldl (fun acc2 kw =>
              (List.range in_c).foldl (fun acc3 ic =>
                let ih := oh * stride.1 + kh
                let iw := ow * stride.2 + kw
                if ih < padding.1 ∨ iw < padding.2 then acc3
                else
                  let realH := ih - padding.1
                  let realW := iw - padding.2
                  if realH ≥ in_h ∨ realW ≥ in_w then acc3
                  else
                    let inVal := input.data.get! (computeFlatIndex inShape [b, realH, realW, ic])
                    let kerVal := kernel.data.get! (computeFlatIndex kerShape [kh, kw, ic, oc])
                    acc3 + inVal * kerVal
              ) acc2
            ) acc
          ) 0.0)
        Except.ok {
          data := data
          shape := Shape.mk' [batch, out_h, out_w, out_c]
          h_data_size := by simp [Array.size_ofFn]
          refcount := RefCount.init
          cow := CowState.init
        }

theorem Tensor.conv2d_requires_4d (input kernel : Tensor)
    (stride padding : Nat × Nat) (h : input.shape.dims.length ≠ 4) :
    ∃ e, Tensor.conv2d input kernel stride padding = Except.error e := by
  unfold Tensor.conv2d; simp [h]
```

```text
(defun make-position-ids (n start)
  (declare (xargs :guard (and (natp n) (natp start))
                  :measure (nfix n)))
  (if (zp n)
      nil
    (cons start (make-position-ids (- n 1) (+ start 1)))))

(defthm nat-listp-of-make-position-ids
  (implies (and (natp n) (natp start))
           (nat-listp (make-position-ids n start)))
  :hints (("Goal" :induct (make-position-ids n start))))

(defthm len-of-make-position-ids
  (implies (natp n)
           (equal (len (make-position-ids n start)) n))
  :hints (("Goal" :induct (make-position-ids n start))))

(defun token-type-ids (tokens segment-id)
  (declare (xargs :guard (and (nat-listp tokens) (natp segment-id))
                  :measure (len tokens)))
  (if (atom tokens)
      nil
    (cons segment-id (token-type-ids (cdr tokens) segment-id))))

(defthm nat-listp-of-token-type-ids
  (implies (and (nat-listp tokens) (natp segment-id))
           (nat-listp (token-type-ids tokens segment-id)))
  :hints (("Goal" :induct (token-type-ids tokens segment-id))))

(defthm len-of-token-type-ids
  (implies (nat-listp tokens)
           (equal (len (token-type-ids tokens segment-id))
                  (len tokens)))
  :hints (("Goal" :induct (token-type-ids tokens segment-id))))

(defun make-input-triple (st text max-len)
  (declare (xargs :guard (and (mgt-state-p st) (stringp text) (natp max-len))))
  (let* ((raw-tokens (encode-with-bos-eos st text))
         (tokens (pad-or-truncate raw-tokens max-len))
         (mask (attention-mask-from-tokens tokens))
         (positions (make-position-ids (len tokens) 0))
         (type-ids (token-type-ids tokens 0)))
    (list tokens mask positions type-ids)))
```
